This discernable trend is called evolutionary trend (You will study the details in Class XII).\nIn this chapter, you are being introduced to morphology and anatomy of frog.\nMorphology refers to the study of form or externally visible features. In the case of plants or microbes, the term morphology precisely means only this.\nIn the case of animals, this refers to the external appearance of the organs or parts of the body.\nThe word anatomy conventionally is used for the study of morphology of internal organs in animals.\nYou will learn the morphology and anatomy of frog, representing vertebrates.\n",

    ],
    "mastery_recommendation": "reinforce_hierarchy_with_analogies",
    "misconception_feedback": null,
    "correct_answer_reasoning": "The correct hierarchy is cell → tissue → organ → organ system. Each level integrates simpler units to perform complex functions: cells are the basic unit, similar cells form tissues, different tissues cooperate in organs, and organs with related functions form systems."
